        </div><div class="casAbstract">Graphene has been widely used as conformal nanobuilding blocks to improve the electrochem. performance of layered metal sulfides (MoS2, WS2, SnS, and SnS2) as anode materials for sodium-ion batteries.  However, it still lacks in-depth understanding of the synergistic effect between these layered sulfides and graphene, which contributes to the enhanced electroactivity for sodium-ion batteries.  Here, MoS2/reduced graphene oxide (RGO) nanocomposites with intimate two-dimensional heterointerfaces are prepd. by a facile one-pot hydrothermal method.  The heterointerfacial area can be effectively tuned by changing the ratio of MoS2 to RGO.  When used as anode materials for sodium-ion batteries, the synergistic effect contributing to the enhanced reversible capacity of MoS2/RGO nanocomposites is closely related with the heterointerfacial area.  The computational results demonstrate that Na prefers to be adsorbed on MoS2 in the MoS2/RGO heterostructure rather than intercalate into the MoS2/RGO heterointerface.  Interestingly, the MoS2/RGO heterointerfaces can significantly increase the electronic cond. of MoS2, store more Na ions, while maintaining the high diffusion mobility of Na atoms on MoS2 surface and high electron transfer efficiency from Na to MoS2.  It is expected that the efforts to establish the correlation between the two-dimensional heterointerface and the electrochem. sodium-ion storage performance offer fundamental understanding for the rational design of layered metal sulfides/graphene composites as high-performance electrode materials for sodium-ion batteries.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGpB50PmkRDAvrVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgCkhVYQ4nK1A"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhsVansbY%253D&amp;md5=3d82ce10422e6d348a48b628852d1b2b</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref47"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref47" class="rightTabRefNumLink">47</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit47" data-doi="10.1002/adma.201306314"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Qu, B.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ma, C.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ji, G.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Xu, C.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Xu, J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Meng, Y.         (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2014</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">26</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">23</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">3854-3859</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">ADVMEW</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0935-9648</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Wiley-VCH Verlag GmbH &amp; Co. KGaA</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">A SnS2-RGO composite with excellent electrochem. performance was prepd. as the anode of sodium ion batteries.  The SnS2-RGO electrode demonstrated a high charge specific capacity (630 mAh g-1 at 0.2 A g-1), good rate performance (544 mAh g-1 at 2 A g-1) and long cycle-life (500 mAh g-1 at 1 A g-1 for 400 cycles).  The excellent electrochem. performance could categorically be attributed to the SnS2 layered structure where the increased interlayer spacing could better accommodate the vol. change in Na-Sn insertion and deinsertions; and the good cond. and mech. resilience of RGO nanocomposites.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGr7HpF3cVbIRLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgCkhVYQ4nK1A"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2cXltFKrsLw%253D&amp;md5=22ee7083d10dd044eeddfd38300681c3</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref48"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref48" class="rightTabRefNumLink">48</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit48" data-doi="10.1016/j.nanoen.2012.07.010"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Xie, J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Liu, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Cao, G.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhu, T.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhao, X.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Self-Assembly of CoS<sub>2</sub>/Graphene Nanoarchitecture by a Facile One-Pot Route and Its Improved Electrochemical Li-Storage Properties</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Nano Energy</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2013</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">2</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">49</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">56</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.nanoen.2012.07.010</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit48R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">48</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Self-assembly of CoS2/graphene nanoarchitecture by a facile one-pot route and its improved electrochemical Li-storage properties</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Xie, Jian; Liu, Shuangyu; Cao, Gaoshao; Zhu, Tiejun; Zhao, Xinbing</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Nano Energy</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2013</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">2</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">1</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">49-56</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">NEANCA</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2211-2855</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier Ltd.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">A CoS2/graphene nanoarchitecture was synthesized by a facile one-step hydrothermal route using graphite oxide, thioacetamide, and CoCl2·6H2O as the starting materials.  The growth of CoS2 and the redn. of the graphite oxide occur simultaneously.  CoS2 nanocrystals with a size of 100-150 nm are uniformly anchored on the both sides of the graphene nanosheets, forming a unique CoS2/graphene hybrid nanostructure.  The electrochem. tests showed that the nanocomposite exhibits obviously enhanced Li-storage properties compared with bare CoS2.  The improvement in electrochem. properties could be attributed to the formation of two-dimensional conductive networks, homogeneous dispersion and immobilization of CoS2 nanoparticles, and the enhanced wetting of active material with the electrolyte by in situ introduced graphene nanosheets.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqQ002Ks8OkLLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgCkhVYQ4nK1A"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC3sXhsV2isL8%253D&amp;md5=31452f6f4d5b46e663858d107f289ca1</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref49"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref49" class="rightTabRefNumLink">49</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit49" data-doi="10.1016/j.carbon.2007.02.034"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Stankovich, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Dikin, D. A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Piner, R. D.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kohlhaas, K. A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kleinhammes, A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Jia, Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wu, Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Nguyen, S. T.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ruoff, R. S.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Synthesis of Graphene-Based Nanosheets Via Chemical Reduction of Exfoliated Graphene oxide</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Carbon</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2007</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">45</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">1558</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">1565</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.carbon.2007.02.034</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref50"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref50" class="rightTabRefNumLink">50</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit50" data-doi="10.1021/nn203393d"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yang, Z.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yao, Z.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Li, G.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Fang, G.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Nie, H.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Liu, Z.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhou, X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Chen, X. a.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Huang, S.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Sulfur-Doped Graphene as an Efficient Metal-Free Cathode Catalyst for Oxygen Reduction</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">ACS Nano</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2012</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">6</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">205</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">211</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/nn203393d</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit50R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">50</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Sulfur-Doped Graphene as an Efficient Metal-free Cathode Catalyst for Oxygen Reduction</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Yang, Zhi; Yao, Zhen; Li, Guifa; Fang, Guoyong; Nie, Huagui; Liu, Zheng; Zhou, Xuemei; Chen, Xi'an; Huang, Shaoming</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">ACS Nano</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2012</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">6</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">1</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">205-211</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">ANCAC3</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1936-0851</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">American Chemical Society</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Tailoring the electronic arrangement of graphene by doping is a practical strategy for producing significantly improved materials for the O-redn. reaction (ORR) in fuel cells (FCs).  Recent studies proved that the C materials doped with the elements, which have the larger (N) or smaller (P, B) electroneg. atoms than C such as N-doped C nanotubes (CNTs), P-doped graphite layers and B-doped CNTs, also showed pronounced catalytic activity.  Herein, the graphenes doped with the elements, which have the similar electronegativity with C such as S and Se, can also exhibit better catalytic activity than the com. Pt/C in alk. media, indicating that these doped graphenes hold great potential for a substitute for Pt-based catalysts in FCs.  The exptl. results are believed to be significant because they not only give further insight into the ORR mechanism of these metal-free doped C materials, but also open a way to fabricate other new low-cost NPMCs with high electrocatalytic activity by a simple, economical, and scalable approach for real FC applications.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqWQqbSkhy1lbVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgCkhVYQ4nK1A"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC3MXhs1OjtbrN&amp;md5=e5861429d3b9a9dbb423b3c96fd22c05</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref51"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref51" class="rightTabRefNumLink">51</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit51" data-doi="10.1002/advs.201500195"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Qie, L.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Chen, W.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Xiong, X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Hu, C.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zou, F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Hu, P.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Huang, Y.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Sulfur-Doped Carbon with Enlarged Interlayer Distance as a High-Performance Anode Material for Sodium-Ion Batteries</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Adv. Science</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">2</span><span class="NLM_elocation-id">1500195</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1002/advs.201500195</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes-1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i10">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/acsami.5b12148" class="ext-link">10.1021/acsami.5b12148</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Schematic of the FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG fabrication procedures; XRD patterns of raw FeSe<sub>2</sub> and FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG prepared at 185 °C for 9, 12, and 15 h, and the comparison of the XRD patterns of raw SG, raw FeSe<sub>2</sub>, and FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG prepared at 185 °C for 12 h; Raman spectra of GO and FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG composites; ex situ XRD patterns of FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG electrode tested at the current density of 500 mA g<sup>–1</sup> in the first cycle at different states; cyclic voltammogram curves of the raw FeSe<sub>2</sub> and the FeSe<sub>2</sub>/G electrode at a scan rate of 0.2 mV s<sup>–1</sup> between 0.01 and 2.5 V and the galvanostatic charge/discharge profiles of the raw FeSe<sub>2</sub> and FeSe<sub>2</sub>/G electrode within the first three cycles at a current density of 500 mA g<sup>–1</sup>; cycle performances of the FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG, FeSe<sub>2</sub>/G, and raw FeSe<sub>2</sub> electrode at a current density of 500 mA g<sup>–1</sup> based on the whole mass of composites in electrode; FESEM images of FeSe<sub>2</sub> and FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG electrode before and after 100 cycles; cycle performance of the G and SG electrodes at a current density of 500 mA g<sup>–1</sup>; cycle performance of the FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG, raw FeSe<sub>2</sub> (64 wt %), and FeSe<sub>2</sub> (80 wt %) electrodes at the current density of 500 mA g<sup>–1</sup>; electrochemical impedance spectra of FeSe<sub>2</sub>/SG and FeSe<sub>2</sub> electrode for SIBs after first cycle (<a href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.5b12148/suppl_file/am5b12148_si_001.pdf" class="ext-link">PDF</a>)</p></li></ul><p></p><div class="supInfoBoxOnFTP "><div class="sup-info-attachments"><ul><li><a class="suppl-anchor" href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.5b12148/suppl_file/am5b12148_si_001.pdf">am5b12148_si_001.pdf (2.21 MB)</a></li></ul></div></div><div id="rightTab-figshare-widget"></div><br><div class="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight" data-pb-dropzone="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight"><div data-widget-def="UX3HTMLWidget" data-widget-id="b84e6b6c-b4d0-4427-b286-3cf14d52d013" class="mb-4">

        <script nonce="90da8bc26cadb325-SJC">
(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

<script nonce="90da8bc26cadb325-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

)|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(a.substr(0,4))) check = true;})(navigator.userAgent||navigator.vendor||window.opera);
              return check;
        };

    var _isMobile = window.mobilecheck();
    if (_isMobile) {
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').addClass('mobile');
    }

    var emailValid = "",
        time = 3000,
        btnStatus = true,
        errorStatus = false,
        errormessage = "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

    function init() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>

var currentJournal = "ACS Applied Materials &amp;amp; Interfaces";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
